***трещать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>треща́ть</a> (5112)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Apparently from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треск.html>треск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tresk</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, with iotation. The same root appears in the related verbs <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трескаться.html>тре́скаться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tréskatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trésnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>треща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">treščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:треснуть.html>тре́снуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to crackle <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">make a fizzing sound</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>меня́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голова.html>голова́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>трещи́т</a></b> (<a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:боль.html>бо́ли</a>)</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u menjá golová <b>treščít</b> (ot bóli)</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I have a splitting headache; my head is ready to burst</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>треща́т</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мороз.html>моро́зы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>treščát</b> morózy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is a biting frost</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to chirr <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">make a trilled sound</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chatter, to jabber</li>
<li>to crack, to be on the point of collapse
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трещать.html>треща́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:шов.html>шва́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>treščátʹ</b> po švam</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fall apart at the seams</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***трещинка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трещинка.html>тре́щинка</a> (21440)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещина.html>тре́щина</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tréščina</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещинка.html>тре́щинка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tréščinka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещинка.html>тре́щинки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещинка.html>тре́щинки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трещинка.html>тре́щинок</a></b>)
</p>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_4">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tri</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>three (3)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></b></i>, in the nominative case or accusative case, even in compounds (23, 33, 43, 103, etc.), governs various forms of the corresponding noun and intervening adjective or adjectival participle. See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dva</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for more information.
</p>

***трибуна.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трибуна.html>трибу́на</a> (4573)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">tribūnus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трибуна.html>трибу́на</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tribúna</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трибуна.html>трибу́ны</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трибуна.html>трибу́ны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трибуна.html>трибу́н</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>podium, platform, rostrum, tribune</li>
<li>stand (for spectators)</li></ol>

***тридцатилетний.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцатилетний.html>тридцатиле́тний</a> (14410)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trídcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-i-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лето.html>ле́то</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">léto</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ний</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцатилетний.html>тридцатиле́тний</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tridcatilétnij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> thirty-year
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцатилетний.html>тридцатиле́тнее</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:царствование.html>ца́рствование</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tridcatilétneje</b> cárstvovanije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>thirty-year</b> reign</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>thirty-year-old
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцатилетний.html>тридцатиле́тняя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:женщина.html>же́нщина</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tridcatilétnjaja</b> žénščina</i> ― <span class="e-translation">a woman <b>of thirty</b>; a <b>thirty-year-old</b> woman</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тридцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a> (744)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-дцать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-dcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or "thrice ten".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trídcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thirty (30)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tridcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trídcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>thirty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>тридцатью́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>tridcatʹjú</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with <b>thirty</b> boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тридцать.html>три́дцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>trídcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>thirty</b> boys</span></div></li></ul>

***трижды.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трижды.html>три́жды</a> (4857)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-жды</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ždy</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трижды.html>три́жды</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tríždy</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>three times, thrice, on three occasions
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трижды.html>три́жды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жи́зни</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tríždy</b> v žízni</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three times</b> in someone's life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>3x, three times as much
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трижды.html>три́жды</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пять.html>пять</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:пятнадцать.html>пятна́дцать</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tríždy</b> pjatʹ — pjatnádcatʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three times</b> five is fifteen</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***тринадцать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:тринадцать.html>трина́дцать</a> (6323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tri</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дцать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, or "three on ten". The final syllable <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">дцать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">dcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is an old short form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:десять.html>де́сять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">désjatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тринадцать.html>трина́дцать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trinádcatʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>thirteen (13)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:тринадцать.html>трина́дцать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trinadcatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in the nominative case and accusative case governs the genitive plural of the noun. In other cases, it governs the corresponding plural case of the noun.
</p>
<ul><li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:тринадцать.html>трина́дцать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trinádcatʹ</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">thirteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тринадцать.html>трина́дцатью</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиками</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>trinádcatʹju</b> málʹčikami</i> ― <span class="e-translation">with thirteen boys</span></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:тринадцать.html>трина́дцать</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>trinádcatʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately thirteen boys</span></div></li></ul>

***триста.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>три́ста</a> (2936)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*tri</i> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sъta</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral_3">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>три́ста</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trísta</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>three hundred (300)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The Russian number <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>три́ста</a></b></i> in the nominative case governs the genitive plural of the noun.<i></i>
</p>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>три́ста</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trísta</b> málʹčikov</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three hundred</b> boys</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мальчик.html>ма́льчиков</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>три́ста</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">málʹčikov <b>trísta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">approximately <b>three hundred</b> boys</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>три́ста</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>кни́г</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>trísta</b> knig</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three hundred</b> books</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>они́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>свои́х</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:триста.html>трёхста́х</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:солдат.html>солда́тах</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Oní govoríli o svoíx <b>trjoxstáx</b> soldátax.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">They were talking about their <b>three hundred</b> soldiers.</span></div></dd></dl>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">трёхсотле́тний</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">trjoxsotlétnij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***трогать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a> (2428)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the same root as Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">trahō</i> according to Goryaev, which would be Proto-Indo-European <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*tregʰ-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">drag</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">treat</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">trace</i>, and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">traction</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trógatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тронуть.html>тро́нуть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to touch</li>
<li>to move <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">emotionally</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to bother, to annoy, to disturb</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start moving</li></ol>

</tbody></table><br>Глагол<h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="<a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a>">Значение</span></h4>
<ol><li>прикасаться, как правило, с целью получения тактильных ощущений <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Ей всего-то и хотелось любоваться красивыми растениями, ухаживать за ними, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">трогать</span> иногда руками и вдыхать их запахи... </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:переносной.html>переносно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a>">перен.</span> эмоционально воздействовать, волновать, беспокоить <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Происходящее в общественной жизни страны, разумеется, не могло не <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">трогать</span> её, отличницу-школьницу, а затем студентку, но он до сих пор ни разу не слышал от неё ни слова одобрения, ни слова осуждения. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:переносной.html>переносно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a>">перен.</span> причинять неудобство кому-либо <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Майор Котлов не велел меня <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">трогать</span>, приказал даже выдать какие-то деньги — за командировку. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Но Соня встала на защиту пьяного обормота и велела его не <b>трогать</b>. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li><span style="font-style: italic;background-color:CCFFFF;cursor:help;" title="<a href = vnd.unilang:переносной.html>переносно́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>значе́ние</a>">перен.</span> браться за что-то, брать что-то <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"> — Как ты смел <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">трогать</span> портфель в моём кабинете, — сказал он, вводя меня за собой в маленькую диванную. </span></li>
</ul></li>


<li>стартовать, отъезжать, начинать движение <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black"> — Можно <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">трогать</span>? — осведомляется Лев Николаевич, держа вожжи. </span></li>
</ul></li>

</ol>
<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="<a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a>">Синонимы</span></h4>
<ol><li>задевать, касаться, прикасаться, соприкасаться, дотрагиваться, притрагиваться</li>
<li>волновать</li>
</ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trógatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогаться.html>тро́гаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">trógatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тронуться.html>тро́нуться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start (for), to get moving, to be off</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to go nuts</li>
<li>to be touched, to be moved (emotionally)</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трогать.html>тро́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">trógatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***трое.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>трое</a> (1071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">tróje</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>three (in a group together), three of them
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>дете́й</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tróje</b> detéj</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three</b> children</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часо́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tróje</b> časóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three</b> watches</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tróje</b> očkóv</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three</b> pairs of glasses</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>на́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>tróje</b> iz nás</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>three</b> of us</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мы.html>нас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:трое.html>тро́е</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nas býlo <b>tróje</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there were <b>three</b> of us</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>The nominative of a collective numeral governs the genitive plural of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. The other cases agree with that of the noun, pronoun, or adjective. Not used with feminine nouns. Used mostly when speaking of children and with pluralia tantum, such as <a href = vnd.unilang:час.html>часы́</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a>, or with pronouns.
</p>
